Style Resolution (CSS → ComputedStyle)\\n**File**: `third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/style_resolver.h`\\n**Class**: `StyleResolver`\\nThe StyleResolver class is responsible for resolving CSS styles for DOM elements. It takes element information and the document's stylesheets and produces a ComputedStyle. The key method is `ResolveStyle()` which takes an Element and returns the computed style. There is a 1-1 relationship between StyleResolver and Document.\\n\\n### 2. Layout Tree (ComputedStyle → LayoutObject)\\n**File**: `third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/layout_object.h`\\n**Class**: `LayoutObject`\\nThe LayoutObject is the base class for the layout tree. Each LayoutObject corresponds to a DOM node that generates boxes in the layout tree. LayoutObject is responsible for performing layout calculations and managing the geometric properties (position, size, margins, etc.) of rendered content. It extends GarbageCollected and implements DisplayItemClient interface. The layout tree is built based on computed styles produced by StyleResolver.\\n\\n### 3. Painting Layer Abstraction (LayoutObject → PaintLayer)\\n**File**: `third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/paint_layer.h`\\n**Class**: `PaintLayer`\\nPaintLayer provides an abstraction for the painting system, creating a tree that mirrors parts of the LayoutObject tree. Not all LayoutObjects have associated PaintLayers - they are created selectively based on CSS properties and positioning context. PaintLayer encapsulates painting state and manages rendering of self-painting layers. Each PaintLayer has an associated LayoutBoxModelObject.\\n\\n### 4. Paint Recording (PaintLayer → DisplayItemList)\\n**Files**: \\n- `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h` (PaintController)\\n- `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/display_item_list.h` (DisplayItemList)\\n\\n**Classes**: `PaintController` and `DisplayItemList`\\n\\nThe PaintController class is responsible for processing display items as they are produced during the paint phase. It maintains a DisplayItemList which is a container for paint operations (DisplayItems) of various types. The DisplayItemList records the actual drawing operations that will be rasterized. PaintController handles caching, cache invalidation, and merging of paint operations.\\n\\n### Pipeline Flow\\nCSS Change → StyleResolver (resolves to ComputedStyle) → LayoutObject tree construction → PaintLayer tree creation → PaintController records DisplayItems into DisplayItemList → Rasterization\\n\\nThis hierarchical structure allows Chromium to efficiently manage the complex process of transforming CSS styles into pixel data while maintaining performance through caching and incremental updates.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":7955,"cache_read_input_tokens":63472,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":7955},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e867e24c-b812-4a5f-83f6-3da3485d822c","uuid":"0dd659fe-4925-43cc-a56b-26f40a251383"}

Paint Recording (PaintLayer → DisplayItemList)\\n**Files**: \\n- `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h` (PaintController)\\n- `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/display_item_list.h` (DisplayItemList)\\n\\n**Classes**: `PaintController` and `DisplayItemList`\\n\\nThe PaintController class is responsible for processing display items as they are produced during the paint phase. It maintains a DisplayItemList which is a container for paint operations (DisplayItems) of various types. The DisplayItemList records the actual drawing operations that will be rasterized. PaintController handles caching, cache invalidation, and merging of paint operations.\\n\\n### Pipeline Flow\\nCSS Change → StyleResolver (resolves to ComputedStyle) → LayoutObject tree construction → PaintLayer tree creation → PaintController records DisplayItems into DisplayItemList → Rasterization\\n\\nThis hierarchical structure allows Chromium to efficiently manage the complex process of transforming CSS styles into pixel data while maintaining performance through caching and incremental updates.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
